<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgang.html>opgang</a> (63612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">opganc</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">op-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a></i> and a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgaan.html>opgaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgang.html>opgang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgang.html>opgangen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgang.html>opgangetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> of a heavenly body (such as the sun or moon)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> (of a country's or a person's power)</li>
<li>staircase</li>
<li>path leading upwards</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgave.html>opgave</a> (21266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgeven.html>opgeven</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgave.html>opgave</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgaven.html>opgaven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgave.html>opgavetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>task, assignment</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgave.html>opgave</a></strong>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgeven.html>opgeven</a> (2031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgeven.html>opgeven</a></strong>

<ol><li>to give up</li>
<li>to relinquish</li>
<li>to report, let know</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:opgeven.html>opgeven</a></b>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i>

***ophoepelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ophoepelen.html>ophoepelen</a> (13913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the late 18th century. Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll <a href = vnd.unilang:hoops.html>hoops</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></i> for more on the meaning “to go away”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ophoepelen.html>ophoepelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mildly vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a>, to go away, to piss off
<ul><li><b>1798</b>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>Brief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Bonifacius Veredik, <a href = vnd.unilang:aangaande.html>aangaande</a> zyn <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:burger.html>burger</a> Minutieux, <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> D ****.", <i>Vaderlandsche letteroefeningen</i>, page 410.

***opkijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opkijken.html>opkijken</a> (9634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opkijken.html>opkijken</a></strong>
</p><p><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To look (in an) up(ward manner); to <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a> one's <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>used with '<a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> ...': to ...)</i> To admire, respect, look up to someone in a <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> position</li></ol>
